<t>CREATE TABLE customers (id INT PRIMARY KEY, name VARCHAR(50), email VARCHAR(50), phone VARCHAR(15), address VARCHAR(100))

CREATE TABLE orders (order_id INT PRIMARY KEY, customer_id INT, order_date TIMESTAMP, order_total DECIMAL(10,2), FOREIGN KEY (customer_id) REFERENCES customers(id))</t><s>UPSERT INTO customers (id, name, email, phone, address) VALUES (1, 'John Doe', 'johndoe@example.com', '1234567890', '123 Main St') ON CONFLICT (id) DO UPDATE SET name = 'John Doe', email = 'johndoe@example.com', phone = '1234567890', address = '123 Main St';</s>

<t>CREATE TABLE customers (
    customer_id INT PRIMARY KEY,
    customer_name VARCHAR(100) NOT NULL,
    email VARCHAR(100) UNIQUE,
    phone_number VARCHAR(20)
);


CREATE TABLE orders (
    order_id INT PRIMARY KEY,
    customer_id INT REFERENCES customers(customer_id),
    order_date DATE,
    total_amount DECIMAL(10, 2) NOT NULL
);


CREATE TABLE products (
    product_id INT PRIMARY KEY,
    product_name VARCHAR(100) NOT NULL,
    price DECIMAL(10, 2) NOT NULL
);
</t><s>UPSERT INTO customers (customer_id, customer_name, email, phone_number) VALUES (1, 'John Doe', 'john.doe@example.com', '1234567890') ON DUPLICATE KEY UPDATE customer_name = VALUES(customer_name), email = VALUES(email), phone_number = VALUES(phone_number);</s>
<t>CREATE TABLE customers (
    customer_id INT PRIMARY KEY,
    customer_name VARCHAR(100) NOT NULL,
    email VARCHAR(100) UNIQUE,
    phone_number VARCHAR(20)
);


CREATE TABLE orders (
    order_id INT PRIMARY KEY,
    customer_id INT REFERENCES customers(customer_id),
    order_date DATE,
    total_amount DECIMAL(10, 2) NOT NULL
);


CREATE TABLE products (
    product_id INT PRIMARY KEY,
    product_name VARCHAR(100) NOT NULL,
    price DECIMAL(10, 2) NOT NULL
);
</t><s>upsert into customers (customer_id, customer_name, email, phone_number) values (1, 'john doe', 'john.doe@example.com', '1234567890') on duplicate key update customer_name = values(customer_name), email = values(email), phone_number = values(phone_number);</s>

    product_id SERIAL PRIMARY KEY,
    product_name VARCHAR(50) NOT NULL,
    price NUMERIC(10, 2) NOT NULL,
    description TEXT
);

CREATE TABLE orders (
    order_id SERIAL PRIMARY KEY,
    customer_id INT REFERENCES customers(customer_id),
    order_date DATE,
    total_amount NUMERIC(10, 2),
    status VARCHAR(20)
);

    transaction_id SERIAL PRIMARY KEY,
    order_id INT REFERENCES orders(order_id),

    payment_method VARCHAR(20)

<t>CREATE TABLE customers (
    customer_id SERIAL PRIMARY KEY,
    customer_name VARCHAR(50) NOT NULL,
    email VARCHAR(100),
    phone_number VARCHAR(15),
    address VARCHAR(255)
);

CREATE TABLE transactions (
    transaction_id SERIAL PRIMARY KEY,
    order_id INT REFERENCES orders(order_id),
    transaction_date TIMESTAMP,
    payment_method VARCHAR(20)
);

CREATE TABLE contacts (
    contact_id SERIAL PRIMARY KEY,
    customer_id INT REFERENCES customers(customer_id),
    contact_name VARCHAR(50) NOT NULL,
    contact_email VARCHAR(100),
    contact_phone VARCHAR(15)
);

    customer_name VARCHAR(50) NOT NULL,
    email VARCHAR(100),
    phone_number VARCHAR(15),
    address VARCHAR(255)
);</t><s>INSERT INTO customers (customer_name, email, phone_number, address) VALUES ('John Doe', 'john.doe@example.com', '1234567890', '123 Main St') ON CONFLICT (customer_name) DO UPDATE SET email = EXCLUDED.email, phone_number = EXCLUDED.phone_number, address = EXCLUDED.address;</s>
<t>CREATE TABLE products (
    product_id SERIAL PRIMARY KEY,
    product_name VARCHAR(50) NOT NULL,
    price NUMERIC(10, 2) NOT NULL,
    description TEXT
);

CREATE TABLE orders (
    order_id SERIAL PRIMARY KEY,
    customer_id INT REFERENCES customers(customer_id),
    order_date DATE,
    total_amount NUMERIC(10, 2),
    status VARCHAR(20)
);

CREATE TABLE transactions (
    transaction_id SERIAL PRIMARY KEY,
    order_id INT REFERENCES orders(order_id),
    transaction_date TIMESTAMP,
    payment_method VARCHAR(20)
);

CREATE TABLE contacts (
    contact_id SERIAL PRIMARY KEY,
    customer_id INT REFERENCES customers(customer_id),
    contact_name VARCHAR(50) NOT NULL,
    contact_email VARCHAR(100),
    contact_phone VARCHAR(15)
);

CREATE TABLE customers (
    customer_id SERIAL PRIMARY KEY,
    customer_name VARCHAR(50) NOT NULL,
    email VARCHAR(100),
    phone_number VARCHAR(15),
    address VARCHAR(255)
);</t><s>insert into customers (customer_name, email, phone_number, address) values ('john doe', 'john.doe@example.com', '1234567890', '123 main st') on conflict (customer_name) do update set email = excluded.email, phone_number = excluded.phone_number, address = excluded.address;</s>

    customer_id INT REFERENCES customers(customer_id),
    contact_name VARCHAR(50) NOT NULL,
    contact_email VARCHAR(100),
    contact_phone VARCHAR(15)
);

CREATE TABLE orders (
    order_id SERIAL PRIMARY KEY,
    customer_id INT REFERENCES customers(customer_id),
    order_date DATE,
    total_amount NUMERIC(10, 2),
    status VARCHAR(20)
);</t><s>INSERT INTO orders (customer_id, order_date, total_amount, status) VALUES (1, '2022-01-01', 100.00, 'Pending') ON CONFLICT (customer_id, order_date) DO UPDATE SET total_amount = EXCLUDED.total_amount, status = EXCLUDED.status;</s>
<t>CREATE TABLE customers (
    customer_id SERIAL PRIMARY KEY,
    customer_name VARCHAR(50) NOT NULL,
    email VARCHAR(100),

    address VARCHAR(255)

    product_id SERIAL PRIMARY KEY,
    product_name VARCHAR(50) NOT NULL,
    price NUMERIC(10, 2) NOT NULL,

);

CREATE TABLE transactions (
    transaction_id SERIAL PRIMARY KEY,
    order_id INT REFERENCES orders(order_id),
    transaction_date TIMESTAMP,
    payment_method VARCHAR(20)
);

    customer_id INT REFERENCES customers(customer_id),
    order_date DATE,
    total_amount NUMERIC(10, 2),
    status VARCHAR(20)
);

    customer_id INT REFERENCES customers(customer_id),
    contact_name VARCHAR(50) NOT NULL,
    contact_email VARCHAR(100),
    contact_phone VARCHAR(15)
);

CREATE TABLE customers (
    customer_id SERIAL PRIMARY KEY,
    customer_name VARCHAR(50) NOT NULL,
    email VARCHAR(100),
    phone_number VARCHAR(15),
    address VARCHAR(255)
);

    customer_id INT REFERENCES customers(customer_id),
    contact_name VARCHAR(50) NOT NULL,
    contact_email VARCHAR(100),
    contact_phone VARCHAR(15)
);

CREATE TABLE orders (
    order_id SERIAL PRIMARY KEY,
    customer_id INT REFERENCES customers(customer_id),
    order_date DATE,
    total_amount NUMERIC(10, 2),
    status VARCHAR(20)
);

CREATE TABLE customers (
    customer_id SERIAL PRIMARY KEY,
    customer_name VARCHAR(50) NOT NULL,
    email VARCHAR(100),
    phone_number VARCHAR(15),
    address VARCHAR(255)
);

CREATE TABLE products (
    product_id SERIAL PRIMARY KEY,
    product_name VARCHAR(50) NOT NULL,
    price NUMERIC(10, 2) NOT NULL,
    description TEXT
);</t><s>insert into orders (customer_id, order_date, total_amount, status) values (1, '2022-01-01', 100.00, 'pending') on conflict (customer_id, order_date) do update set total_amount = excluded.total_amount, status = excluded.status;</s>

    customer_id INT REFERENCES customers(customer_id),
    contact_name VARCHAR(50) NOT NULL,
    contact_email VARCHAR(100),
    contact_phone VARCHAR(15)
);

CREATE TABLE orders (
    order_id SERIAL PRIMARY KEY,
    customer_id INT REFERENCES customers(customer_id),
    order_date DATE,
    total_amount NUMERIC(10, 2),
    status VARCHAR(20)
);

CREATE TABLE customers (
    customer_id SERIAL PRIMARY KEY,
    customer_name VARCHAR(50) NOT NULL,
    email VARCHAR(100),
    phone_number VARCHAR(15),
    address VARCHAR(255)
);

CREATE TABLE transactions (
    transaction_id SERIAL PRIMARY KEY,
    order_id INT REFERENCES orders(order_id),
    transaction_date TIMESTAMP,
    payment_method VARCHAR(20)
);

CREATE TABLE products (
    product_id SERIAL PRIMARY KEY,
    product_name VARCHAR(50) NOT NULL,
    price NUMERIC(10, 2) NOT NULL,
    description TEXT
);</t><s>INSERT INTO orders (customer_id, order_date, total_amount, status) VALUES (1, '2022-01-01', 100.00, 'Pending') ON CONFLICT (customer_id, order_date) DO UPDATE SET total_amount = EXCLUDED.total_amount, status = EXCLUDED.status;</s>

    transaction_id SERIAL PRIMARY KEY,

    payment_method VARCHAR(20)
);

    order_id INT REFERENCES orders(order_id),
    transaction_date TIMESTAMP,
    payment_method VARCHAR(20)
);

CREATE TABLE contacts (
    contact_id SERIAL PRIMARY KEY,
    customer_id INT REFERENCES customers(customer_id),
    contact_name VARCHAR(50) NOT NULL,
    contact_email VARCHAR(100),
    contact_phone VARCHAR(15)
);

CREATE TABLE products (
    product_id SERIAL PRIMARY KEY,
    product_name VARCHAR(50) NOT NULL,
    price NUMERIC(10, 2) NOT NULL,
    description TEXT
);

CREATE TABLE customers (
    customer_id SERIAL PRIMARY KEY,
    customer_name VARCHAR(50) NOT NULL,
    email VARCHAR(100),
    phone_number VARCHAR(15),
    address VARCHAR(255)
);

CREATE TABLE orders (
    order_id SERIAL PRIMARY KEY,
    customer_id INT REFERENCES customers(customer_id),
    order_date DATE,
    total_amount NUMERIC(10, 2),
    status VARCHAR(20)
);</t><s>insert into contacts (customer_id, contact_name, contact_email, contact_phone) values (1, 'jane smith', 'jane.smith@example.com', '9876543210') on conflict (customer_id, contact_name) do update set contact_email = excluded.contact_email, contact_phone = excluded.contact_phone;</s>

    customer_id INT REFERENCES customers(customer_id),
    order_date DATE,
    total_amount NUMERIC(10, 2),
    status VARCHAR(20)
);

CREATE TABLE products (
    product_id SERIAL PRIMARY KEY,
    product_name VARCHAR(50) NOT NULL,
    price NUMERIC(10, 2) NOT NULL,
    description TEXT
);</t><s>insert into contacts (customer_id, contact_name, contact_email, contact_phone) values (1, 'jane smith', 'jane.smith@example.com', '9876543210') on conflict (customer_id, contact_name) do update set contact_email = excluded.contact_email, contact_phone = excluded.contact_phone;</s>
<t>CREATE TABLE contacts (
    contact_id SERIAL PRIMARY KEY,
    customer_id INT REFERENCES customers(customer_id),
    contact_name VARCHAR(50) NOT NULL,
    contact_email VARCHAR(100),
    contact_phone VARCHAR(15)
);

CREATE TABLE transactions (
    transaction_id SERIAL PRIMARY KEY,
    order_id INT REFERENCES orders(order_id),
    transaction_date TIMESTAMP,
    payment_method VARCHAR(20)
);
